		function initialize() {

			var styles = [
			{
			  stylers: [
				{ hue: "#537b89" },
				{ saturation: -20 }
			  ]
			},{
			  featureType: "road",
			  elementType: "geometry",
			  stylers: [
				{ lightness: 100 },
				{ visibility: "simplified" }
			  ]
			},{
			  featureType: "road",
			  elementType: "labels",
			  stylers: [
				{ visibility: "off" }
			  ]
			}
			];
		  
			var styledMap = new google.maps.StyledMapType(styles, {name: "Csodálatos Magyarország helyek"});

			var mapOptions = {
				center: new google.maps.LatLng(47.1810693,19.6713543),
				zoom: 9,
				zoomControl: true,
				zoomControlOptions: {position: google.maps.ControlPosition.LEFT_CENTER},
				mapTypeControlOptions: {
					mapTypeIds: [google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP, 'map_style']
				}	  
			};

			map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('mapcanvas'), mapOptions);
			map.mapTypes.set('map_style', styledMap);
			map.setMapTypeId('map_style');

			infoWindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow();
			google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'click', function() {
				infoWindow.close();
			});

			displayMarkers();
		}
		google.maps.event.addDomListener(window, 'load', initialize);

		function displayMarkers(){

		   var bounds = new google.maps.LatLngBounds();
		   for (var i = 0; i < markersData.length; i++){

		      var latlng = new google.maps.LatLng(markersData[i].lat, markersData[i].lng);
		      var name = markersData[i].name;
		      var address1 = markersData[i].address1;
		      var address2 = markersData[i].address2;
		      var postalCode = markersData[i].postalCode;
		      createMarker(latlng, name, address1, address2, postalCode);
		      bounds.extend(latlng);  
		   }

		   map.fitBounds(bounds);
		}

		// This function creates each marker and it sets their Info Window content

		function createMarker(latlng, name, address1, address2, postalCode){
			var iconBase = 'https://csodalatosmagyarorszag.hu/wp-content/themes/csm2022/i/';
		    var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
		      position: latlng,
		      map: map,
			  icon: iconBase + 'balaton_map_icon.png',
		      title: name
		   });

		   google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() {

		      var iwContent = '<div id="iw_container" class="ac">' +
		         '<div class="iw_title">' + address1 + '</div>' +
		         '<div class="iw_content">' +
		         '<h2 class="ttu">' + address2 + '</h2> ' +
		         postalCode + '</div></div>';
		      
		      infoWindow.setContent(iwContent);
		      infoWindow.open(map, marker);
		   });
		}
		</script>

	</div>
	</div>
</main>

<script type="text/javascript">

    function ChangeUrl(page, url) {
        if (typeof (history.pushState) != "undefined") {
            var obj = { Page: page, Url: url };
            history.pushState(obj, obj.Page, obj.Url);
        } else {
            console.log("Browser does not support HTML5.");
            return false;
        }
    }

	jQuery(document).ready(function($){

		//Add or update get parameter

		function updateQueryStringParameter(uri, key, value) {
		  var re = new RegExp("([?&])" + key + "=.*?(&|$)", "i");
		  var separator = uri.indexOf('?') !== -1 ? "&" : "?";
		  if (uri.match(re)) {
			return uri.replace(re, '$1' + key + "=" + value + '$2');
		  }
		  else {
			return uri + separator + key + "=" + value;
		  }
		}

		function removeURLParameter(url, parameter) {
		  var urlParts = url.split('?');

		  if (urlParts.length >= 2) {
		    // Get first part, and remove from array
		    var urlBase = urlParts.shift();

		    // Join it back up
		    var queryString = urlParts.join('?');

		    var prefix = encodeURIComponent(parameter) + '=';
		    var parts = queryString.split(/[&;]/g);

		    // Reverse iteration as may be destructive
		    for (var i = parts.length; i-- > 0; ) {
		      // Idiom for string.startsWith
		      if (parts[i].lastIndexOf(prefix, 0) !== -1) {
		        parts.splice(i, 1);
		      }
		    }

		    url = urlBase + '?' + parts.join('&');
		  }

		  return url;
		}

		$('#video_banner_mute').click(function (e) {

			this.classList.toggle('muted')
			theVideo.classList.toggle('muted')
			//console.log(theVideo.muted)
			//$("video").prop('muted', true)

		})

		// Programok/Esemenyek forms


			$('select.select2').select2({
			    dropdownAutoWidth : true,
			    width: '100%'
			});

			function collect_form() {

				if ($('#program_kategoriak').length) {
					// Programok
					var kategoria_url = $('#program_kategoriak').val();
				} else {
					// Galeriak
					var kategoria_url = location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname;

				}

				var final_url=kategoria_url;
				//console.log(final_url);
				var telepules = $('#program_telepulesek').val();
				var cimke = $('#program_cimke').val();

		  		var full_url=window.location.href;
				var url = new URL(full_url);
				var idoszak = url.searchParams.get("idoszak");
				var map = url.searchParams.get("map");
				
				if (telepules && telepules!="all") {final_url=updateQueryStringParameter(final_url,'telepules',telepules);} else {final_url=removeURLParameter(final_url, 'telepules');}
				if (idoszak) {final_url=updateQueryStringParameter(final_url,'idoszak',idoszak);} else {final_url=removeURLParameter(final_url, 'idoszak');}
				if (map) {final_url=updateQueryStringParameter(final_url,'map',map);} else {final_url=removeURLParameter(final_url, 'map');}
				if (cimke && cimke!="all") {final_url=updateQueryStringParameter(final_url,'cimke',cimke);} else {final_url=removeURLParameter(final_url, 'cimke');}

				console.log(final_url);

				if (final_url=="") {
					window.location.href=location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname;
				} else {
					window.location.href=final_url;
				}

			}

			$("select.select_program").change(function() {
				collect_form();		
			});


		var lastScrollTop = 0;
		// element should be replaced with the actual target element on which you have applied scroll, use window in case of no target element.
		window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){ // or window.addEventListener("scroll"....
		   var st = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop; // Credits: "https://github.com/qeremy/so/blob/master/so.dom.js#L426"
		   if (st > lastScrollTop){
			   // downscroll code
			   //$('div.head').hide();
		   } else {
			  // upscroll code
			  //$('div.head').show();
		   }
		   lastScrollTop = st;
		}, false);
		
		window.onscroll = function(){
			  if (window.pageYOffset<360) {
				//stick on
				if (jQuery("body").hasClass("stickyhome")) {jQuery("body").removeClass("stickyhome");}
			  } else {
				  //sticky off
				  if (jQuery("body").hasClass("stickyhome")) {} else {jQuery("body").addClass("stickyhome");}
			  }
		};

		
		//mobil menu
		//$('#nav').slicknav({prependTo: '#menu', label: '<i class="triple-wave"></i>'});
		
		//Swipebox
		$("a[rel='swipebox'], dl.gallery-item a").swipebox({useCSS:true, useSVG:false});

		//owl slider
		jQuery(document).ready(function($){
		  $("#topswapper").owlCarousel({
			items:1,
			loop: true,
			autoplay: true,
			dots: false,
			autoplayHoverPause: true,
			slideBy: 'page',
			navText: '',
			smartSpeed: 1000
		  });		  
			$('#topswappercontrols .owl-next').click(function() {$('#topswapper').trigger('next.owl.carousel');})
			$('#topswappercontrols .owl-prev').click(function() {$('#topswapper').trigger('prev.owl.carousel');})			
		});

		$(".the_menu_trigger").on('click', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			$(`body`).removeClass(`menu_open`);
			$("#the_fs_menu").slideToggle(250);
		});

		$(".searching").on('click', function() {
			$("#sf").slideToggle(250);
		});

		$(".searchingd, .searchingclose").on('click', function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#sfd").slideToggle(250);
		});

		// mobile menu

		$('#nav_mobile_trigger').click(function(ev){
			ev.preventDefault();
			$(`body`).toggleClass(`menu_open`);
			$("div.subheader").slideToggle(250);		
		});

		//tabs

		$('ul.tabs li').click(function(){
			var tab_id = $(this).attr('data-tab');

			$('ul.tabs li').removeClass('current');
			$('.tab-content').removeClass('current');

			$(this).addClass('current');
			$("#"+tab_id).addClass('current');
		})


		// registration checked

		$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1) input[type=radio]').click(function(){
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').addClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').removeClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').addClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').addClass('unselected');		
		})

		$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2) input[type=radio]').click(function(){
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').addClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').removeClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').addClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').addClass('unselected');		
		})

		$( "li.nemek" ).find("input").parent().addClass('unselected');
		$( "li.nemek" ).find("input:checked").parent().removeClass('unselected');
		$( "li.nemek" ).find("input:checked").parent().addClass('selected');

		$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3) input[type=radio]').click(function(){
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').addClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(3)').removeClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(1)').addClass('unselected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').removeClass('selected');
			$('li.nemek li:nth-child(2)').addClass('unselected');		
		})

	    });

		$('ul.tabbed.selection_4 li a').click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {return;}
			var whereto=$(this).attr('data-tab');
			$('#tab_contents div.tab_content').addClass('dn');
			$('#'+whereto).removeClass('dn');
			$('ul.selection_4.tabbed li a').removeClass('active');
			$(this).addClass('active');
		});


	$('input#datepickerfromto').daterangepicker({
		autoUpdateInput: true,
		autoApply: true,
			locale: {
			'format': "YYYY/MM/DD",
			'cancelLabel' : 'Törlés',
			'monthNames': [
				'Január',
				'Február',
				'Március',
				'Április',
				'Május',
				'Június',
				'Július',
				'Augusztus',
				'Szeptember',
				'Október',
				'November',
				'December'
			],
			'daysOfWeek': [
				'Va',
				'Hé',
				'Ke',
				'Sze',
				'Cs',
				'Pé',
				'Szo'
			],
			  "firstDay": 1
		}
	},function(start, end, label) {
  		var start_date=start.format('YYYYMMDD');
  		var end_date=end.format('YYYYMMDD');

  		var final_parameters="";
		var loc_protocol=location.protocol+ '//';
		var loc_host=location.host;
  		var loc_pathname=location.pathname;
  		var the_base_url=loc_protocol+loc_host+loc_pathname;
  		var full_url=window.location.href;

		var url = new URL(full_url);
		var idoszak = start_date+'_'+end_date;
		var telepules = url.searchParams.get("telepules");
		var map = url.searchParams.get("map");

  		if (idoszak) {final_parameters=updateQueryStringParameter(final_parameters,'idoszak',idoszak);} else {final_parameters=removeURLParameter(final_parameters, 'idoszak');}
  		if (telepules) {final_parameters=updateQueryStringParameter(final_parameters,'telepules',telepules);} else {final_parameters=removeURLParameter(final_parameters, 'telepules');}
  		if (map) {final_parameters=updateQueryStringParameter(final_parameters,'map',map);} else {final_parameters=removeURLParameter(final_parameters, 'map');}
		
		the_final_url=loc_protocol+loc_host+loc_pathname+final_parameters;


		window.location.href=the_final_url;

	});

	});	
	</script>
